      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Rosie" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Rosie" href="/user/show/1269587-rosie">Rosie</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1269587-rosie?shelf=books-i-own">books-i-own</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer25425816" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2415527727638927854">I do enjoy James Herbert's books but this one does fall a bit flat in retrospect. <br/><br/>James Herbert creates likeable characters and intriguing suspense with relaistic and believable fantasy. I do, however, think that he plugs in the gaps with non-stop sex scenes - Nell and Thom twiceish, Nell and the other guy, Nell and Katie, Thom and Jennet twice. Sex does play a large part of the plot especially in regards to Nell and Thom, as she is trying to seduce him for other means. <br/><br/>The ending is where James</span>
  <span id="freeText2415527727638927854" style="display:none">I do enjoy James Herbert's books but this one does fall a bit flat in retrospect. <br /><br />James Herbert creates likeable characters and intriguing suspense with relaistic and believable fantasy. I do, however, think that he plugs in the gaps with non-stop sex scenes - Nell and Thom twiceish, Nell and the other guy, Nell and Katie, Thom and Jennet twice. Sex does play a large part of the plot especially in regards to Nell and Thom, as she is trying to seduce him for other means. <br /><br />The ending is where James Herbert falls down. The entire book builds up this suspense for this almighty battle, hypes it up as <i>the</i> battle between good and evil and where everything will change etc. And then we have the climax with an enemy we can't even look at or "he'll own your soul" who doesn't even bother with Thom, and the main character who is supposed to be the hero, spends the entire time hiding underneath his newly found Undine girlfriend. Not exactly the Apocalypse we'd been sold all those damn pages ago! <br /><br />And the motives for the whole conflict...are we supposed to believe that people turn to dark magick and supposed "Wicca", conjure up terrible creatures to steal your enemy's semen so you can curse him to death...all over the allotment of estate in an old man's Will?<br /><br />A good book, worth a read, but the absence of a proper plot, real motives for the conflict and a satisfying conclusion is apparent despite Herbert's attempt to distract the reader with erotic scenes - "Look over there! A lesbian sex scene!" - and isn't really worth much after the first read.</span>
  <a data-text-id="2415527727638927854" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Gav451" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Gav451" href="/user/show/6110708-gav451">Gav451</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer815933677" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7458815836799348871">The one that got away:<br/><br/>The last few James Herbert books I read were really good. Thoughtful, interesting, atmospheric and pacey. This one however seems to have gotten away from him a little. <br/><br/>On consideration 3 may be one too many stars. The problem is the plot is ever so slightly thin and the sex scenes are jarringly out of place within the story. They serve no purpose other than to allow the cover of the copy I read to assert that it was a dark erotic fantasy.<br/><br/>When I was a young teenager the earl</span>
  <span id="freeText7458815836799348871" style="display:none">The one that got away:<br /><br />The last few James Herbert books I read were really good. Thoughtful, interesting, atmospheric and pacey. This one however seems to have gotten away from him a little. <br /><br />On consideration 3 may be one too many stars. The problem is the plot is ever so slightly thin and the sex scenes are jarringly out of place within the story. They serve no purpose other than to allow the cover of the copy I read to assert that it was a dark erotic fantasy.<br /><br />When I was a young teenager the early books were just what I needed. Pacey stories about loads of grisly deaths. Quite easy to read but making me feel 'edgy' like I was rebelling slightly while reading. I have a lot of affection for James Herbert books because of that and i loved the fact that his books were getting better and better.<br /><br />Lets consider this a slip then, a momentary lapse of concentration. I did read it to the end so it cannot have been all bad and there were elements within the book I really enjoyed and which could have been utilised more and expanded on but as a whole I felt like this book got distracted by the sex and forgot the plot.</span>
  <a data-text-id="7458815836799348871" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('IMqqi9vu07vMyAmPNksnCfqqcyoxxs9cxyf5sdBtjLlBsrfqnpZw5JQpz6C3QX4gNqS4Za5BrSc4zLdt0o6yqg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('hUn1lvp3tBPdHd+VN+lRVB39nG+3rqtSpOSc/20Km9fkMej3vw8XTIX8Gbq24wh90fNXICgpySlbD9Ijb+mlxA==')})
  }

      <div id="aboutAuthor" class=" clearFloats bigBox"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground"><a href="/author/show/80984.James_Herbert">About James Herbert</a></h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent">
          <div class='bookAuthorProfile'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__topContainer'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__photoContainer'>
<a href="/author/show/80984.James_Herbert"><div class='bookAuthorProfile__photo' style='background-image: url(https://images.gr-assets.com/authors/1395179325p3/80984.jpg);'></div>

<a href="/author/show/80984.James_Herbert">James Herbert
</a></div>

1,734
followers

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer679207420097135212">James Herbert was Britain's number one bestselling writer (a position he held ever since publication of his first novel) and one of the world's top writers of thriller/horror fiction. <br/><br/>He was one of our greatest popular novelists, whose books are sold in thirty-three other languages, including Russian and Chinese. Widely imitated and hugely influential, his 19 novels have sold more than 42 million </span>
  <span id="freeText679207420097135212" style="display:none">James Herbert was Britain's number one bestselling writer (a position he held ever since publication of his first novel) and one of the world's top writers of thriller/horror fiction. <br /><br />He was one of our greatest popular novelists, whose books are sold in thirty-three other languages, including Russian and Chinese. Widely imitated and hugely influential, his 19 novels have sold more than 42 million copies worldwide. <br /><br />As an author he produced some of the most powerful horror fiction of the past decade. With a skillful blend of horror and thriller fiction, he explored the shaded territories of evil, evoking a sense of brooding menace and rising tension. He relentlessly draws the reader through the story's ultimate revelation - one that will stay to chill the mind long after the book has been laid aside. His bestsellers, THE MAGIC COTTAGE, HAUNTED, SEPULCHRE, and CREED, enhanced his reputation as a writer of depth and originality. His novels THE FOG, THE DARK, and THE SURVIVOR have been hailed as classics of the genre.</span>
  <a data-text-id="679207420097135212" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

</div>
